  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f240a110-b951-4af3-83d0-ff1c74696506'

<div id="review_1870749425" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1870749425" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1870749425?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/33660250-forbid-me">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=childhood-loves">childhood-loves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=age-difference">age-difference</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1870749425" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7799759288827899610">After reading 'Complicate Me', I couldn't wait to start the next book in the series. M. Robinson's stories have a way of sucking me in. Like it's predecessor, 'Forbid Me' proved to be an emotional, angsty story of forbidden love. I couldn't get enough.<br/><br/>'Forbid Me' is the story of Lucas's little sister, Lily and his best friend, Jacob. Much like half-pint, Lily has always been around the "Good Ol' Boys" for all of her life. Also like half-pint, she was very much "off-limits" to any of the guys. As</span>
  <span id="freeText7799759288827899610" style="display:none">After reading 'Complicate Me', I couldn't wait to start the next book in the series. M. Robinson's stories have a way of sucking me in. Like it's predecessor, 'Forbid Me' proved to be an emotional, angsty story of forbidden love. I couldn't get enough.<br /><br />'Forbid Me' is the story of Lucas's little sister, Lily and his best friend, Jacob. Much like half-pint, Lily has always been around the "Good Ol' Boys" for all of her life. Also like half-pint, she was very much "off-limits" to any of the guys. As much as they sheltered Alex, who was only a couple of years younger than the boys, it was far worse for Lily, who was seven years younger than Jacob.<br /><br />The age-difference between Lily and Jacob might be tough for some to swallow. After all, she was around 15 when they first started exploring their attraction. He was in his early twenties at the time. If Alex was "half-pint", then Lily was "jail bait". <br /><br />Most of the conflict in their story centers upon the forbidden nature of their relationship. In many ways, it was very similar to 'Complicate Me'. Jacob spends a lot of time trying to deny his attraction to Lily because she is so much younger and the sister of his best friend. Eventually, Lily has had enough of Jacob's rejection and tries to move on, only to have him then figure out how much he wants her. Once he's no longer fighting his attraction, they waste time trying to hide it from their friends/family. <br /><br />Where this story differed from 'Complicate Me' was in the personalities of the characters. Lily was no shrinking violet. This was one bold, outspoken heroine. M. Robinson did a great job of crafting her character. She managed to keep her from coming across as young or "victimy", which was essential, given the age difference between her and Jacob. If anything, you felt like she was the one taking advantage of Jacob.<br /><br />Jacob also stood out from Lucas's character. Yes, he was attracted to a younger, off-limits girl, but that was where the similarities ended for me. He didn't engage in the same self-destructive behaviors that Lucas did. He also seemed to give more regard to Lily and her feelings. Sure, he made plenty of mistakes along the way, but there wouldn't have been much of a story otherwise.<br /><br />Overall, this was a great story. It was sweet, taboo and very angsty. I listened to the Audible version and it was well-narrated. If you're looking for a sweet, forbidden love story, this is a good choice.<br /><br />Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7799759288827899610" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1409877734" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1409877734" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1409877734?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1409877734" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15091952437415863792"><b>4-4.5 stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/99B71EE0-F7FE-4B66-92A1-485C2284F4B3_zpscjqh4mbv.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448376562i/17131768._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 99B71EE0-F7FE-4B66-92A1-485C2284F4B3_zpscjqh4mbv.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>After reading <i>Complicate Me</i>, I had to get my hands on Lily and Jacob’s story. A brother's best friend story- which is one of my favorite types of stories to read. I love the forbidden aspect of these types of books. Lily and Jacob’s story started when she was 15. Jacob is 7 years older than she is. The problem isn’t just the age difference, no it’s much more than that. The problem is that Lily’s older brother, Lucas, is Jacob’s best friend. No matter how old Lily is, it will neve</span>
  <span id="freeText15091952437415863792" style="display:none"><b>4-4.5 stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/99B71EE0-F7FE-4B66-92A1-485C2284F4B3_zpscjqh4mbv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448376562i/17131768._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 99B71EE0-F7FE-4B66-92A1-485C2284F4B3_zpscjqh4mbv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After reading <i>Complicate Me</i>, I had to get my hands on Lily and Jacob’s story. A brother's best friend story- which is one of my favorite types of stories to read. I love the forbidden aspect of these types of books. Lily and Jacob’s story started when she was 15. Jacob is 7 years older than she is. The problem isn’t just the age difference, no it’s much more than that. The problem is that Lily’s older brother, Lucas, is Jacob’s best friend. No matter how old Lily is, it will never be okay that they’re together. <br><br>This story goes back and forth from past to present, with both Lily and Jacob’s point of view.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/D2577372-195D-473A-9F53-E42BB30C477D_zpssx3oflwv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448376562i/17131769._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo D2577372-195D-473A-9F53-E42BB30C477D_zpssx3oflwv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lily has wanted Jacob for as long as she could remember. And she’s always known that he’s had feelings for her, he just can never go there. He’s older and he doesn’t want to risk his friendship with Lucas. But sometimes, feelings and desires are stronger than anything, including friendship and loyalty. Especially when that feeling is love.   In the past, Jacob couldn’t push Lily far enough away. And she couldn’t get close enough to him. Now, years later, after so much has happened, things have changed. They both are in different places in their lives and want different things. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Choose us. I promise I won’t ever walk away from you. from us again. I promise to give you all of me, forever. I’m all in, sweet girl, damn the fucking consequences.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/FC304AF0-3739-4532-8DF0-B6EC5601D40B_zpske39vbjn.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448376562i/17131770._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo FC304AF0-3739-4532-8DF0-B6EC5601D40B_zpske39vbjn.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved getting all the background of Lily and Jacob, watching them fight their feelings for each other. And the present, watching Lily start to trust Jacob again and watching their love grow and come together. I just waited and waited for that moment that I knew was going to happen! And I was nervous as heck waiting! <br><br>M. Robinson writes angsty very well. She has been able to write two books in this series that I haven’t been able to put down. I had to know what was going to happen next and how things were going to turn out. That is probably the best quality in a story. Being unable to put it down. After reading the epilogue to this story, once again I am left dying for the next one. I’m so excited to see what happens with Dylan’s story!!! Even though this could technically be read as a stand-alone, due to the characters connections and all the background of these boys, I would highly recommend you read in order. If you love a steamy, angsty and forbidden story- pick this one up! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/73D24181-6E7C-4268-9330-11F5A97E02C1_zpsfjrkprmy.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448376562i/17131771._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 73D24181-6E7C-4268-9330-11F5A97E02C1_zpsfjrkprmy.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </span>

<div id="review_1398098751" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1398098751" />
    <a title="Pam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13865261-pam"><img alt="Pam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374039144p2/13865261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1398098751?book_show_action=true">Sep 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pam" href="/user/show/13865261-pam">Pam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/27207913-forbid-me">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=5">5</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=love-story">love-story</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=fucked-up-n-broken">fucked-up-n-broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=second-chances-love-n-life">second-chances-love-n-life</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=sixty-first-reads">sixty-first-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1398098751" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1465243630388392100"><i>4.5 it will be our little secret stars</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448528272i/17155929.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><b>❤❤Jacob & Lily❤❤</b><br/><br/>This is their story of <i>then</i> and <i>now</i>, the long uphill battle to get to their HEA, taking you to hell and back. It was never a question as to if they were meant to be, after all they are each others lobster, it was all just a matter of finding the right time. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442893839i/16290546._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>For Jacob, his whole world was Lily, so when he turned his back and left, he left a piece of himself in her care...she just doesn't know it yet. She has his heart, his love and his soul; </span>
  <span id="freeText1465243630388392100" style="display:none"><i>4.5 it will be our little secret stars</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448528272i/17155929.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b>❤❤Jacob &amp; Lily❤❤</b><br><br>This is their story of <i>then</i> and <i>now</i>, the long uphill battle to get to their HEA, taking you to hell and back. It was never a question as to if they were meant to be, after all they are each others lobster, it was all just a matter of finding the right time. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442893839i/16290546._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For Jacob, his whole world was Lily, so when he turned his back and left, he left a piece of himself in her care...she just doesn't know it yet. She has his heart, his love and his soul; and now that fate has crossed their paths, nothing will stop him from getting her back...even if he has to breakdown each brick she's built around her broken-wounded heart.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I was her first and I would be her last.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448528272i/17155930._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For Lily, she wants nothing more than for him to leave her alone so she can continue living her life. In three years she managed to do fine all by herself, doing what she loves and never letting anyone close. When she sees him, all the pain and heart ache comes rushing back, actually if she was honest with herself, it never even left. Her mind protects her heart, but her heart knows the truth; she is and always be his. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I. HATE. YOU,"<br><br>“No you don’t,” he growled. “You don’t hate me at all, baby. What you hate is that you still love me.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Actions speak louder than words, so with each passing day he shows her just how much he truly loves her...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448528272i/17155931._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>reminding her just who her body belongs too...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I get to strip you completely naked. I get to make you wet. I get to taste you. I get to make you come. It’s mine. Do you understand me?” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448528272ra/17155932.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>it's them against the world, pretty soon they have to come out of their little cocoon and face the ones who <i>forbid</i> their love.<br><br>Like with all of M. Robinson's novels, she effortlessly blends the past and the present, making you feel as if you are living each moment with each character. For me, my love for Jacob and Lily began in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25701594.Complicate_Me__The_Good_Ol__Boys___1_" title="Complicate Me (The Good Ol' Boys, #1) by M. Robinson" rel="nofollow noopener">Complicate Me</a>, and while these are considered stand alone reads, it gives you added history if you read it first. <br><br>There were moments I felt hatred, others where I unknowingly held my breath waiting for the other shoe to drop while at the same time hoping for no more heart ache. I won't lie, my favorite parts all took place in the "now", because it was the closest to their HEA. The angst that I have grown accustomed to getting with any or M. Robinson's books was felt, but to my surprise at a lower scale. <br><br>Jacob is charming to fault, he is sweet with a sometimes cheesy demeanor, has an utterly delicious dirty mouth, and the skills to back it up. Lily was a mix of sweet and sassy, we watched her grow through the pages and while her love for Jacob was clear as day, it matured with age. Their age difference never bothered me, maybe because my hubby and I are in the same boat, I'm a firm believer that age is nothing but a number and you really can't put an age on love. Regardless of it all, I loved it, I loved them and I can't wait to see Dylan and Aubrey's story, this from the looks of it will be one hell of a ride. <br><br>This is a definite recommended read especially for those who love a them-against-the-world kind of read, an alpha male who isn't afraid to get on his knees to say I'm sorry, and a love story that spans a lifetime. <br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by the author, via *Sixty First Reads*, in exchange for an honest review.</i><br> <br>***Quotes above are taken from the ARC version of the book and may differ upon publication.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1465243630388392100" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1661734905" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1661734905" />
    <a title="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books"><img alt="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528808758p2/37314676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1661734905?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" href="/user/show/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books">NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=romance-young-adult-etc">romance-young-adult-etc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=college">college</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1661734905" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14926590438050824167"><b>
  <i>***4,5 "<u>Your lobster!</u>" stars***</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465740464i/19395571._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Hurting you is my biggest regret, loving you is my only redemption.” </i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Yes!!! Karma is a bitch, Jacob!!!</i><br/>And yes, I'm still mad with Jacob because he was standing between Lucas and Alex, but damn me, i liked his story very much!!! Even though that he was a fuckin' hypocrite... <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465386494ra/19349038.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>And why i'm saying that???</i><br/>Well, this was the story of Jacob, one of Alex's Good Ol' Boys and Lily's, Lucas's baby sister who was seven years older than Jacob...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395572.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Do you see the irony here</i></span>
  <span id="freeText14926590438050824167" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>***4,5 "<u>Your lobster!</u>" stars***</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465740464i/19395571._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“Hurting you is my biggest regret, loving you is my only redemption.” </i>
</b><br><br><i>Yes!!! Karma is a bitch, Jacob!!!</i><br>And yes, I'm still mad with Jacob because he was standing between Lucas and Alex, but damn me, i liked his story very much!!! Even though that he was a fuckin' hypocrite... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465386494ra/19349038.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>And why i'm saying that???</i><br>Well, this was the story of Jacob, one of Alex's Good Ol' Boys and Lily's, Lucas's baby sister who was seven years older than Jacob...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395572.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Do you see the irony here??? And why karma is a bitch???</i><br><br><b>
  <i>"I've always loved you, but that doesn’t change the fact that this is wrong. What we’re doing, what we’ve been doing since you were fifteen behind everyone’s backs is fucking wrong."</i>
</b><br><br>From the last chapter of the previous book, i was eager to see what it will happen to this book and as in the previous book, the prologue made me wild to learn how the things will end up for Jacob and Lily... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395573.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>For once again, we had back and fourth to past and present but i liked the way it happened...<br><br><b>
  <i>"Have you ever wanted something so badly that it consumed your very being? Something that you could practically taste on your tongue? Something that was all you thought about, day in and day out? <br>The feeling is so intense that it becomes a part of you. You could feel it under your skin, in your heart, consuming your mind.<br>That was Jacob to me.<br>He was my core.<br>I couldn’t remember a time when I didn’t want him.<br>When I didn’t think about him.<br>When I didn’t love him."</i>
</b><br><br>Lily fell in love with Jacob in a very young age... He was her brother's best friend and they always had a special connection even though that they were 7 years apart...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395574.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Jacob started to acknowledge Lily's presence as a woman when she was fifteen and even though that he tried to stay away from her, there were times that he wasn't so strong to put some distance between them and Lily was a little shit who knew how to play him...<br>But those facts didn't make him to not hurt her and stay away from her for a long time...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395575.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I’m hurting you when I’m with you, and I’m hurting you when I’m not. I can’t fucking win either way."</i>
</b><br><br>At the "present" <i>(not exactly!)</i>, Jacob is determined to get Lily back because he can't live anymore without her, but Lilly was hurt and angry and he made his life miserable.... <br>She is making him to work really, really hard to earn her back...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395576.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“You’ve loved me your entire life. I’m in your skin. I’m in your blood. I’m in your heart.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"I. HATE. YOU,"<br>“No you don’t,” he growled. “You don’t hate me at all, baby. What you hate is that you still love me.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>Will Jacob persuade her that he is telling the truth and that he want to spend the rest of his life with her???<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450920160ra/17485543.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And even though they will back together, are they having a chance to stay together???<br>And what about Lucas???<br>How will he react to this relationship???</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395577.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>“Choose us. I promise I won’t ever walk away from you. from us again. I promise to give you all of me, forever...<br>I’m all in, sweet girl, damn the fucking consequences.”</i>
</b><br><br>I liked Lily and Jacob as a couple...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389543868ra/8039060.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>They had an intense relationship, a perfect chemistry between them, even though that they had seven years apart from each other...<br>Yep, their beginning seemed a little bit wrong, but their feelings were so strong that you could ignore how wrong it seems that she was 15 and he was 22...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458065432ra/18440317.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>In this case, Lucas was one of the main reasons that they stayed apart and they witnessed so much pain, but it wasn't intetional since Lucas had no clue of what it was happening behind his back...<br>To be real, Lily and Jacob lived much more together than Lucas and Alex and their relationship was hot and intense...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424211735ra/13728797.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“I hated that my body wanted one thing and my mind told me another, both at war with each other.<br>My heart.<br>Betraying me once again.<br>It. Wanted. Him.<br>And that… I hated that, too.”</i>
</b> <i>{Lily}</i><br><br><b>
  <i>"I was blinded by her.<br>Consumed by her.<br>Wrecked by her.<br>She owned each and every part of me, right down to my soul.<br>I. Loved. Her."</i>
</b> <i>{Jacob}</i><br><br>I loved Lilly from the first book already...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395578.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>I loved the fact that even though she was so young, she was sooo intuitive...<br>She understood the love between Alex and Lucas and her heart was breaking for their behalf...<br>I liked Lily because she was a spitfire... A fiesty little thing that always spoke her mind even though the others were disagreeing with her...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395579.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She was real, authentic, with a big mouth and a huge heart...<br>She was full of life, until she felt a double loss and she lost her shiny side... But not for too long!!!<br>Jacob was everything she wanted in her life, but he kept hurting her and she couldn't bare it anymore... But even though everything that happened between them, she never stopped loving him and that was scaring her!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390783070ra/8277478.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"As much as I hated to admit it, he was right. I didn’t see a future until Jacob came back into the picture and that scared me more than anything. I was jumping right back in. Head first into being dependent on him, and I had yet to figure out if it was a good or bad thing."</i>
</b><br><br>Jacob was a little bit rough around the edges... He was very different from Lucas...<br>He was an alpha male, a little bit dominant on bed and he was very determined... especially toward Lilly. As the rest of the Good Ol' Boys, he was a little bit of caveman and very possessive of his woman...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395580.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>To be honest, i never fully forgive him for his part on the first story.<br>I was so mad that he couldn't watch his own goddamn business and what is really pissing me off is the fact that he wasn't innocent... He was doing something worse behind everyone's back!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395581.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But i have to admit that with Lily, he was very sweet and determined...<br>He was truly loving her and he made everything in his power to shoe her how much she means to him... He could do anything for Lily to take him back and i appreciated his efforts!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395582.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"She was my home.<br>So pure, so innocent, so angelic.<br>So mine.<br>She possessed my thoughts.<br>She owned my heart.<br>She fueled my wants and desires."</i>
</b><br><br>Yes, for once again, i loved that i saw the rest of the gang and I loved that i saw the happiness of Alex and Lucas... They deserved a piece of heaven after everything that got through...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465740464ra/19395583.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Also my curiosity about Dylan and Aubrey hit another level... I'm dying to find out what the hell happened between them even though that it is obvious that they are still loving each other after all those years and I can't understand why she is with that piss of shit, Jeremy and why she is allowing him to treat her in that awful way...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438367036ra/15698949.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>And that epilogue???</i>
</b> Damn, it made me wild to start the next book immediately...<br></span>

<div id="review_1447947404" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1447947404" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1447947404?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-couples">best-couples</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=girl-power">girl-power</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1447947404" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16158847529097697426"><b><br/>★5 Forbidden Stars! ★<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448591586i/17163662.jpg' width='“400"' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>"I won't loose you again. You're mine, Lillian."-Jacob</b><br/><br/><b>Forbid Me</b> is the second book in The Good Ol' Boys Series and it was a thrilling read. Lily and Jacob were magical together and every moment with them was simply unforgettable.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448601264i/17164912._SX540_.png' width='“400"' height='100' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>"Have you ever wanted something so badly that it consumed your very being? Something that you could practically taste on your tongue. Something that was all you thought about, day in and day out?"-Lily</b><br/><br/>We met Lily and Jacob in the first book of the se</span>
  <span id="freeText16158847529097697426" style="display:none"><b><br>★5 Forbidden Stars! ★<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448591586i/17163662.jpg" width='“400"' height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>"I won't loose you again. You're mine, Lillian."-Jacob</b><br><br><b>Forbid Me</b> is the second book in The Good Ol' Boys Series and it was a thrilling read. Lily and Jacob were magical together and every moment with them was simply unforgettable.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448601264i/17164912._SX540_.png" width='“400"' height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>"Have you ever wanted something so badly that it consumed your very being? Something that you could practically taste on your tongue. Something that was all you thought about, day in and day out?"-Lily</b><br><br>We met Lily and Jacob in the first book of the series <b>Complicate Me</b>. Lily is Lucas' younger sister and Jacob is Lucas' best friend. Following the theme of the first book in the series, we have a case of "forbidden love". Jacob is seven years older than Lily. Although he should be feeling "brotherly" love for her, when Lily blossoms into a young woman Jacob feels something completely opposite of what a brother should feel for a sister. Additionally, Lily is head over heels in love with Jacob. Can they ever find a way to overcome the age difference and the judgement of their family, and friends?<br><br><b>"Every time I pictured my future, it was always with Lily by my side."-Jacob</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448591586i/17163663.jpg" width='“400"' height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As <b>Forbid Me</b> shifts between the present and the past, we experience the developing friendship between Jacob and Lily and the undeniable attraction they share. Although Jacob tries to do the "honorable" thing, Lily is a vixen that will stop at nothing to be with him. The constant push and pull was invigorating with the intense sexual chemistry building and the continuous battle of the wills between Lily and Jacob! Perhaps one of the most refreshing elements of this read is the tenacity of Lily! Jacob makes plenty of mistakes and when he "comes back" to "claim her", he has to work for it! (Which, might I add, just made the chase even that more exciting!)<br><br><b>"His love fucking consumed me."-Lily</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448591586i/17163664.jpg" width='“400"' height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Both Jacob and Lily are complex characters with a great deal of heart! The fact that they must face circumstances that are continually ripping them apart only makes their reunion that much sweeter! To have a read where both the hero and the heroine are so well matched for one another is like winning the lottery! The passion between these two was smoking hot. <br><br><b>"I want you in my mouth, Lillian. I could taste you in my dream. I woke up knowing what I wanted for breakfast. I want you in my bed."-Jacob</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448591586i/17163665.jpg" width='“400"' height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Told in dual POV, <b>Forbid Me</b> offers a perfect blend of romance and steam. The supporting characters continue to play a vital role in the plot development and enhance each moment with their strong connections to each other. With a well constructed story arc, witty dialogue, and unforgettable characters, this is one read you do not want to miss! <br><br><b>"Just her. Always her."- Jacob</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448591586i/17163666.jpg" width='“400"' height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Just Jacob. Only him."- Lily</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448601264i/17164912._SX540_.png" width='“400"' height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Overall, <b>Forbid Me</b> is more than just a 5 star read. It is a "must drop everything on my TBR shelf" and "read it NOW"! I thoroughly enjoyed every second of it. I have already been back to my kindle to re-read my favorite scenes (several times). Additionally, I will be counting down the days for the next Good Ol' Boy to hit my kindle. Bravo M. Robinson! Bravo! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448592848i/17163941.jpg" width='“400"' height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>***The Good Ol' Boys Series***<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25701594.Complicate_Me__The_Good_Ol__Boys___1_" title="Complicate Me (The Good Ol' Boys, #1) by M. Robinson" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1441291691s/25701594.jpg" alt="Complicate Me (The Good Ol' Boys, #1) by M. Robinson" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26777823.Forbid_Me__The_Good_Ol__Boys___2_" title="Forbid Me (The Good Ol' Boys, #2) by M. Robinson" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1444831002s/26777823.jpg" alt="Forbid Me (The Good Ol' Boys, #2) by M. Robinson" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>~ARC graciously provided via author in exchange for an honest review!~<br><br>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><br><a href="https://craziesrusbookblog.wordpress.com//" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434387282i/15214674._SX540_.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><a href="https://twitter.com/CraziesRus" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1447537998" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1447537998" />
    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1447537998?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=arc-netgalley-request">arc-netgalley-request</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1447537998" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8853077551708433350"><b>Genre: </b> NA Contemporary Romance<br/><b>Type: </b> Standalone Book 2 of The Good Ol’ Boys<br/><b>POV: </b> First Person - Dual<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424140745i/13720990.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448196700i/17108741.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lillian (Lily) Ryder was known as Kid for being the youngest in their group of friends. Always feeling left out and treated like a kid, she yearn to make her mark especially in the eye of certain someone who she had her heart on since she was very young.<br/><br/>Being the oldest of the bunch, Jacob Foster is used of being seen as the brother, But as Lily blossomed into a young woman, every year it</span>
  <span id="freeText8853077551708433350" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b> NA Contemporary Romance<br><b>Type: </b> Standalone Book 2 of The Good Ol’ Boys<br><b>POV: </b> First Person - Dual<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424140745i/13720990.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448196700i/17108741.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lillian (Lily) Ryder was known as Kid for being the youngest in their group of friends. Always feeling left out and treated like a kid, she yearn to make her mark especially in the eye of certain someone who she had her heart on since she was very young.<br><br>Being the oldest of the bunch, Jacob Foster is used of being seen as the brother, But as Lily blossomed into a young woman, every year it became harder to resist her. Out of respect to her brother and his best friend he tried to push her away without realizing he was only hurting himself that way.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423265644i/13602509.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In Book 1, Lily was never really part of the group and I never really paid attention to her, so I’m glad she got her moment in this one. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I didn’t see a future until Jacob came back into the picture and that scared me more than anything.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I love seeing a different side of her, with her fun and flirty demeanor. She was also a free spirit who wasn’t afraid to go after what she wanted.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>She owned each and every part of me, right down to my soul.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Jacob was the responsible one. Having feelings for Lily, made it hard for him to decide whether to do what’s right or what’s best. I love how he put everything on the line to show her how much he wanted her.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448196399ra/17108726.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story went between present and past, from their pre-teen years until their adult life. We got to see how they started as friends and evolved to something more all while keeping it a secret to everyone around them, and how it all fell apart when things were just about to get better.<br><br>What I love the most about the book is how the other characters still played a big part in the couple’s life. I especially like how Alex was a big influence for Lily. However, I feel this book is lacking the emotions that I got from the first book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You’ve loved me your entire life. I’m in your skin. I’m in your blood. I’m in your heart.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I was expecting some major angst but I didn’t feel much of it. I love it when characters suffered and I felt like Jacob and Lily didn’t suffered enough – as in the reasons they were apart were trivial and how they got back together were too effortless. Maybe that’s just me and my sadistic nature lol!<br><br>Forbid Me tells the story of a forbidden romance between friends who became something more and how their relationship affecting those who close to them.<br><br><i><b>Note:</b><br>The next book is of Dylan and from the ending of this book, it looks like it’s going to be explosive. Looking forward to his story :D </i><br><br><b>Standalone books in the series:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25701594.Complicate_Me__The_Good_Ol__Boys___1_" title="Complicate Me (The Good Ol' Boys, #1) by M. Robinson" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1441291691s/25701594.jpg" alt="Complicate Me (The Good Ol' Boys, #1) by M. Robinson" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26777823.Forbid_Me__The_Good_Ol__Boys___2_" title="Forbid Me (The Good Ol' Boys, #2) by M. Robinson" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1444831002s/26777823.jpg" alt="Forbid Me (The Good Ol' Boys, #2) by M. Robinson" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27874214.Dylan___Aubrey__The_Good_Ol__Boys___3_" title="Dylan &amp; Aubrey (The Good Ol' Boys, #3) by M. Robinson" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1448155335s/27874214.jpg" alt="Dylan &amp; Aubrey (The Good Ol' Boys, #3) by M. Robinson" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437991042i/15653385.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:<br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412943984i/11445453.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer11519882342900222582"><b>*****5 Forbidden Stars*****</b><br/><br/><i>(ARC kindly provided by author)</i><br/><br/>Jacob and Lilly's story was everything I hoped for and more. Emotional and tender; this is the tale of a <i>forbidden</i> love, that was able to withstand time and tragedy, but only grew stronger inside the hearts of these amazing characters. <br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/7c7564d9-cdf0-4b07-b57a-31bb9ec9889b_zpsbjxhdzlw.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446658716i/16857668.jpg' alt=' photo 7c7564d9-cdf0-4b07-b57a-31bb9ec9889b_zpsbjxhdzlw.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Lily is Luca's little sister and she's loved Jacob for as long as she can remember. The love and admiration she felt for her brother's best friend her whole life, turned romantic as she grew older. Lily</span>
  <span id="freeText11519882342900222582" style="display:none"><b>*****5 Forbidden Stars*****</b><br><br><i>(ARC kindly provided by author)</i><br><br>Jacob and Lilly's story was everything I hoped for and more. Emotional and tender; this is the tale of a <i>forbidden</i> love, that was able to withstand time and tragedy, but only grew stronger inside the hearts of these amazing characters. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/7c7564d9-cdf0-4b07-b57a-31bb9ec9889b_zpsbjxhdzlw.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446658716i/16857668.jpg" alt=" photo 7c7564d9-cdf0-4b07-b57a-31bb9ec9889b_zpsbjxhdzlw.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lily is Luca's little sister and she's loved Jacob for as long as she can remember. The love and admiration she felt for her brother's best friend her whole life, turned romantic as she grew older. Lily knows with every fiber in her being, that Jacob is her soulmate but he doesn't see her as anything more than his friend's baby sister.<br><br>Jacob is seven years older than Lily and even though he's always had love and a fierce instinct to protect her, he can't fathom the idea of admitting she's something more to him. When Lilly becomes of appropriate age, Jacob struggles with the attraction towards her, because the worse thing a guy can do to his best friend, other than to sleep with his woman and is to date his little sister, and Jacob can't do that to Lucas. So he tries everything, in order to avoid Lily.<br><br>Lily's mom is sick with cancer and the thought of loosing her has Lily struggling with everything in her life, she's so sad and scared and only Jacob feels like a safe haven during those trying times. The love Lily feels for him is the balm the soothes the scars in her heart. Jacob can't handle seeing Lily in pain so he gives her everything in order to help her, problem is when he finds himself forced to take it all away, and brake her heart yet again. <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/image_zpsuvmfhuol.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447780310i/17049520._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsuvmfhuol.jpeg" width="365" height="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jacob goes away to Law school and becomes a very successful lawyer, he made partners and a lot of money but the feeling of loneliness never went away, no matter how much opulence he achieved. He very well knows, he could never truly be happy without Lily in his life but after three years, can he go back and prove to her that she's everything to him and he wants her forever, for real this time?<br><br>When Jacob comes back into her life Lily feels the need to protect her heart more than ever. She's hesitant due to their tumultuous past and she's determined not to make the same mistakes. They both needed the time apart, both of them have grown into the people they were suppose to be but something is always missing in the puzzle that is their lives, would the final piece fit this time? Read this amazing book and find out!!!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/417e8920-6cc3-4b66-b9b6-dcaae9a7363a_zpshr9rnlb2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446658716i/16857669.jpg" alt=" photo 417e8920-6cc3-4b66-b9b6-dcaae9a7363a_zpshr9rnlb2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This novel was so emotional, I cried and got my heart broken along with Lily and even though I was mad at Jacob more than once, I understood his reasoning and his struggles. <br><br>What I loved most about <i>Forbid Me</i> was Lily's strength. Her mother's illness, Jacob's hot and cold behavior, Lily always remained strong through it all. She didn't allow her heartaches to define her. She was set out to do only what she wanted to do, no matter what anybody said, she was her own person and that quality was pretty inspiring to me. Hard times catch to us all, and if in those moments we can find a little bit of Lily inside us, everything should be alright.<br><br>As we read their story we catch up with the rest of the boys and it's impossible not to get excited about what's more to come in this series. M.Robinson created a group of characters with complicated stories that feel so real and as we learn more about them, they will each claim a piece of your heart.<br><br>As we walk along the streets of Oak Island and they become more familiar to us; it will be a place where we'll cry, laugh and fall in love with the <i>Good Ol' Boys...</i><br><br>A must read series that has it all, romance, steam and angst. I loved it!!!!<br><br><br>To Pre-order Forbid Me: <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Forbid-Me-Good-Boys-Book-ebook/dp/B016FWMGGW/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1446658666&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=forbid+me+m+robinson">http://www.amazon.com/Forbid-Me-Good-...</a><br><br>My <i>Forbid Me</i> music playlist: <br>*Nothing Else Matters by Lissie<br>*Games People Play by Lissie <br>* Tennesse Whiskey by Chris Stapleton <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/image.jpg1_zpsgbvgk2qi.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441511882i/16118321.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg1_zpsgbvgk2qi.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1427131430" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5492427483089566781"><i> ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review</i><br/><br/><a href='http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Teasers/92174272f01acb24c58e645a96031c_zpswiopak4w.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/><a href='https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/22546671031/in/dateposted/' title='#fORBIDmE1' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>In this seductively enticing romance, M. Robinson delivers yet again another complicated love story but this time with intricate layers and elements of first love, friendship, family, second chances, forgiveness, new beginnings, and a forbidden romance to get our hearts racing and yearning for more. With her wickedly beautiful and sinful prose, M. Robinson enchants her readers on all facets of love from first crush, first love, hear</span>
  <span id="freeText5492427483089566781" style="display:none"><i> ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Teasers/92174272f01acb24c58e645a96031c_zpswiopak4w.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448038133i/17085224.gif" alt=" photo 92174272f01acb24c58e645a96031c_zpswiopak4w.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/22546671031/in/dateposted/" title="#fORBIDmE1" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446007199i/16734061._SX540_.jpg" width="640" height="333" alt="#fORBIDmE1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In this seductively enticing romance, M. Robinson delivers yet again another complicated love story but this time with intricate layers and elements of first love, friendship, family, second chances, forgiveness, new beginnings, and a forbidden romance to get our hearts racing and yearning for more. With her wickedly beautiful and sinful prose, M. Robinson enchants her readers on all facets of love from first crush, first love, heartbreak, anger, lust, jealousy, and second chances. She sophisticatedly rivets her readers as she reminds readers there is nothing forbidden about love when it's your heart and true love on the line. So can an innocent love blossomed to a forever kind of love? Or will friendship and age be the deciding factor as to why two fated lovers will go on their separate ways? So in this forbidden tale of young love, can two fated mates finally realize that true love isn't meant to be easy? That love doesn't appear on command and it'll put you through hurdles but in the end, none of that will matter because it's about how you overcome these hurdles that will define your love. So can a forbidden love prosper and shatter all the doubts, insecurities, and the people that stands in their way in order to prove that there is nothing forbidden about true love?<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/22347551530/in/photostream/" title="#fORBIDME_3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446007199i/16734062._SX540_.jpg" width="640" height="416" alt="#fORBIDME_3" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Forbid Me</b> is the second installment of <i>The Good Ol' Boys Series</i> and once again, readers are reunited with a group of friends who grew up together and had their lives intertwined. Each moment of their life was ingrained and built on their strong love for each other. And so begins the tale when a friendship gets complicated and blurred, when Jacob Foster begins to start look at his best friend's little sister a little differently. When Jacob first laid eyes on Lilian Ryder, he always saw her and treated her as his little sister that is until when he finally saw a young woman standing before him. Soon Lilian Ryder became the apple of his eyes, the beat to his heart, and the air he breathes. So what happens when the lines of what is right and wrong begins to get blurred? <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/22535455535/in/dateposted/" title="#forbidT" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446007199i/16734063._SX540_.jpg" width="640" height="426" alt="#forbidT" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>The seven year age gap of Lily and Jacob was one of the biggest factor that stood in their way. It was a constant reminder to Jacob that he's toying and walking a fine line with danger especially when he knows and should be seeing her as his best friend's little sister. But when attraction, lust and love soon begins to take precedence, Jacob and Lily find themselves at a crossroad in their relationship. To start something that could lead something so beautiful. Or take a chance on a love that could destroy years of friendship. As they could no longer deny their feelings for one another, how can something so wrong feel so right?<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/22535495505/in/photostream/" title="#fORBIDME" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446007199i/16734064._SX540_.jpg" width="640" height="320" alt="#fORBIDME" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>M. Robinson has truly stepped up and elevated her writing to a whole new level as she delivers a book that was filled with everything that I loved, craved, and wanted in a forbidden romance. Ms. Robinson has sensitively and sophisticatedly delivered a forbidden romance that will set hearts racing as readers realize that the love of Jacob and Lily is something that can't be stopped. I loved that the author was able to make readers FEEL all the raw emotions, heartbreak, and loss of Jacob and Lily as they faced the uphill battle of their relationship. M. Robinson did an amazing job highlighting and showcasing the passion and tangible bond that Jacob and Lily had for each other was built on a solid foundation of love, understanding and respect. Nothing about their love was tainted and forbidden when readers realize, see, and feel their true love coursing through each of the pages. So if you are looking for a book that speaks volumes on love, honesty, vulnerabilities, and second chances then I highly recommend you to read <b>Forbid Me.</b> The only forbidden thing about reading this book is denying yourself to read an epic love story between two fated lovers who were meant to have their lives entangled with one another. <br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Teasers/barel_zpsdsj9yp0u.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448038133i/17085225.gif" alt=" photo barel_zpsdsj9yp0u.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Review can also be found on Four Chicks Flipping Pages: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://fourchicksflippingpages.weebly.com">http://fourchicksflippingpages.weebly...</a></i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7233168.M__Robinson" title="M. Robinson" rel="nofollow noopener">M. Robinson</a></span>

<div id="review_1448051273" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1448051273" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1448051273?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13126896-michelle?shelf=01-signed">01-signed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1448051273" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10020076157902647532">I have to start this with saying that although each of the books in this series focuses on a particular character and can probably be read as a stand-alone, don’t. Read them in order. One of the best part of this series is the buildup. Not just of the current book, but of the next one. <br/><br/>Now excuse me while I freak the fuck out. <br/><br/>The way Complicate Me ended, I knew one thing. I needed this book. Had to have it. Jacob has known Lilian since the day she was born. He loved her from the moment he saw h</span>
  <span id="freeText10020076157902647532" style="display:none">I have to start this with saying that although each of the books in this series focuses on a particular character and can probably be read as a stand-alone, don’t. Read them in order. One of the best part of this series is the buildup. Not just of the current book, but of the next one. <br><br>Now excuse me while I freak the fuck out. <br><br>The way Complicate Me ended, I knew one thing. I needed this book. Had to have it. Jacob has known Lilian since the day she was born. He loved her from the moment he saw her. But that love started to change. That love turned into something that could not be denied even if it was bound to destroy everything. She was just a girl. He was a man. She was his best friend’s little sister. <br><br>Okay so I stayed up until around 4am reading this. I was dying. I had to have all the pieces. I needed to know what happened. How three years had passed without these to seeing or speaking to one another. How did a man in his twenties give into the temptations of a teenage girl? How did they break each other completely? <br><br>This story is told in dual points of view and also with timeline jumps to the past and then back into present day. Each segment of this story was a buildup. Each chapter ending was a mini-little-heart-stopping-cliffhanger. I loved that the author worked in the angst in this manner. The story itself was filled with it. But it wasn’t this fabricated angst that backfires when you become so annoyed with the characters. The story held all of this. The storyline and structure of the book was the key. A fucking brilliant move. Far too many times I struggle with an angsty read when it is forced. This wasn’t forced one bit. I wasn’t told this story was heartbreaking – I knew it because it broke my fucking hear to read it. Everything about this story just flowed so perfectly. The way she didn’t make their relationship sordid at the start. The way she gave you Jacob’s POV and how much he struggled to give into what his heart wanted even if it could cost him everything. <br><br>As much as this gem was a girl falling for her brother’s best friend and an age-taboo romance, it was also a coming of age book. We saw Lily grow, we saw Jacob grow. We saw them struggle with life and the hard stuff, and come out on the other side, scars and all. And boy were these two damaged. <br><br>Then toss in the emotional aspects of this story. A very key part of this story also took place in Complicate Me – from a completely different POV. I knew it was coming. But nothing, NOTHING, could have prepared me for those moments. Jacob in those moments, Lily drowning in her sorrow – that just tore me to shreds. These two had so many obstacles. So many challenges to overcome. <br><br>Forbid Me is a story of second chances. A love story that shows you just how strong the pull of love can be. How sometimes, it can be so wrong and so right at the same time. That nothing is easy. Nothing comes without pain. That sometimes it’s just the right person is there at the wrong time. <br><br>I was on the edge of my seat during this entire experience. I sobbed. I soared. And I loved every fucking minute of the torture. <br><br>I need Dylan’s story. Right. Now. <br><br>This is a must read series. You will not regret it.<br><br><br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/125438022@N06/15250834182" title="ARC by Book Worm, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410813673i/11155676.jpg" width="400" height="166" alt="ARC" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10020076157902647532" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1555456375" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1555456375" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1555456375?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/27207913-forbid-me">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=september-2016">september-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=college-romance">college-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=family-series">family-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=series-book">series-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=high-school">high-school</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1555456375" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7900057285786692282">"Forbid Me" is the second book of the "Good Ol' Boys" series, and the author did a beautiful job at making sure that all of my pet peeves that were present in the first book are now gone in this one!! <br/><br/>This story is about Jacob (who is one of the group of boys that are good friends) and Lily; who is one of the other Good Ol' boys members baby sister. That being said, you can imagine that any kind of attraction between Jacob and Lily has to be hidden, not only because she is Lucas's baby sis; but </span>
  <span id="freeText7900057285786692282" style="display:none">"Forbid Me" is the second book of the "Good Ol' Boys" series, and the author did a beautiful job at making sure that all of my pet peeves that were present in the first book are now gone in this one!! <br /><br />This story is about Jacob (who is one of the group of boys that are good friends) and Lily; who is one of the other Good Ol' boys members baby sister. That being said, you can imagine that any kind of attraction between Jacob and Lily has to be hidden, not only because she is Lucas's baby sis; but also because she is 7 years younger than Jacob. This makes things very tense and forbidden considering Jacob has known her since she has been born. Lily has always been in love with Jacob, and she lets him know it from a very young age. Jacob tries to stay noble for many many years, until the physical attraction starts when Lily becomes 15. The bond these two share is very solid, and yes...it begins very innocent until they both become older. There are a few kisses that take place when she is 15; but Jacob is very good at walking away before things get too out of hand. That is until he one day walks away one too many times, and finds himself trying to live without his soul mate for three years.<br /><br />The other thing I really enjoyed about this book is how we were given a bit of their story in the past, and then in the present. It was alternating time frames through out and I found it worked to make a much smoother story, and one where the angst and the romance were balanced very nicely.<br />Even though we do get glimpses in the past, it doesn't come across too much nor does it over power the story. <br /><br />This series seems to be getting better and better, and I can't wait to start book three, which features Dylan and Aubrey. M. Robinson is a very talented author who is able to keep me glued to each page she has written. I highly recommend this series!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7900057285786692282" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
