<div id="review_1450306468" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1450306468" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1450306468?book_show_action=true">Nov 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1450306468" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14265722203124162589"><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Have you ever wanted something so badly that it consumed your every being? Something that you could practically taste on your tongue? Something that was all you thought about, day in and day out? The feeling so intense that it becomes a part of you. You could feel it under your skin, in your heart, consuming your mind. <br/>That was Jacob to me. </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>I first fell in love with the idea of Jacob and Lily in <i>Complicate Me</i> then I basically stalked M. Robinson waiting for more information. I love b</span>
  <span id="freeText14265722203124162589" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Have you ever wanted something so badly that it consumed your every being? Something that you could practically taste on your tongue? Something that was all you thought about, day in and day out? The feeling so intense that it becomes a part of you. You could feel it under your skin, in your heart, consuming your mind. <br>That was Jacob to me. </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>I first fell in love with the idea of Jacob and Lily in <i>Complicate Me</i> then I basically stalked M. Robinson waiting for more information. I love brother’s best friend stories and I love stories with age gaps, it just makes them a little more forbidden. Lily is Lucas’s younger sister, seven years younger and Jacob is Lucas’s best friend. <br><br>For as long as Lily can remember she has had a crush on her brother’s best friend. He has always been the hot older guy, but as they get older he becomes someone she can rely and lean on. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448324238i/17122582._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jacob doesn’t immediately develop feelings for Lily, but as she gets older he begins to see her in another light. It isn’t planned and he really struggles with his feelings. It isn’t just that he has put Lily on a pedestal he also feels he is just too old for her. He wants Lily to experience life and have normal teenage girl experiences. <br><br>The story is told from alternating POV and alternates between past and present. I love how Robinson told the story with the reflections on the past, but it felt like it was changing so quickly. I think so much of that came from my overwhelming desire to know more about their past. A lot of their relationship was developing secretly going on during <i>Complete Me</i>. The sneaking around and hiding is my favorite parts of these stories. Since it alternated so quickly I was always left wanting more. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448324238i/17122583._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jacob and Lily together isn't easy, even after they are both adults they have so much to overcome. Lily has always been the one chasing Jacob, so Jacob needs to prove his feelings to Lily. I loved seeing Jacob pursue Lily, I love how he made her feel. These characters are easy to love and attach yourself to. You want Lily and Jacob to find happiness. <br><br>This series has quickly become one of my favorites and with every book I look forward to more. Each book features a different “Good Ol’ Boy, regardless I recommend reading them all. I love how addicting these books are and how I am always looking forward to more.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I was blinded by her. Consumed by her. Wrecked by her. She owned each and every part of me, right down to my soul.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. </i>
</b><br><br>

    <a title="Kelli C " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c"><img alt="Kelli C " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1426900480p2/14931216.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelli C " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelli C " href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c">Kelli C </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=must-reads">must-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=steamy-read">steamy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=taboo-love">taboo-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=v-card-intact">v-card-intact</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=fab-writing">fab-writing</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1441506344" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14924732130372247867"><b>4.5 KID Stars!</b> <br/><br/><i>ARC provided generously per author in exchange for honest review</i><br/><br/>M. Robinson is quickly becoming a one click favorite in my love for angst department. I was completely blown away after <i>Complicate Me</i> and beyond rocked when the last written words set up a taboo love story for the ages. To say this book was highly anticipated would be an understatement.<br/><br/>While this book is a standalone, I would 100% recommend reading <i>Complicate Me</i> first to really know the boys and understand the connect</span>
  <span id="freeText14924732130372247867" style="display:none"><b>4.5 KID Stars!</b> <br /><br /><i>ARC provided generously per author in exchange for honest review</i><br /><br />M. Robinson is quickly becoming a one click favorite in my love for angst department. I was completely blown away after <i>Complicate Me</i> and beyond rocked when the last written words set up a taboo love story for the ages. To say this book was highly anticipated would be an understatement.<br /><br />While this book is a standalone, I would 100% recommend reading <i>Complicate Me</i> first to really know the boys and understand the connections established. That being said, Jacob Foster found his "lobster" the moment a young Lillian Ryder got scared to go to the bathroom after a scary movie. The only problem is...7 years separating him from that little girl.<br /><br />M. Robinson did and amazing thing...she made a love story set in the foundation of friendship, protection, and added in taboo desire. What once was a "big brother" type of love turned into a growing fire with passing years of passion driven thoughts and passing looks of longing until the meeting of lips, just once, turns both worlds upside down.<br /><br />Unlike book 1 with the back and forth emotional angst. Jacob and Lily have had their angst. They have a past full of tears, harsh words, and goodbyes that hurt one another deeply. Now it is time to finally grasp onto what was always meant to be. The only problem is...an older, wiser Lily is not the same infatuated little girl that Jacob once cared for. Needing actions over empty words, Lily challenges Jacob to STAY...for once. Hold onto your seats and enjoy the hell out of a man's journey to make Lillian his for all to finally see!<br /><br />I really enjoyed this read, a lot. I think the writing was beyond great and the story flowed so well with using the past told in dual POV's to push the present. I know some may worry about the age difference and cringe at the thought of a college man and a 16 year old girl...DONT! This read is thought provoking as the author makes you realize that love has no boundaries. She shows the struggle with want and need and makes you question your own moral compass. More than that, she shows that love may not be easy...it may not be right...but will it wait???</span>
  <a data-text-id="14924732130372247867" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1409174702" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1409174702" />
    <a title="Olga therebelreader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24443337-olga-therebelreader"><img alt="Olga therebelreader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540920390p2/24443337.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1409174702?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Olga therebelreader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Olga therebelreader" href="/user/show/24443337-olga-therebelreader">Olga therebelreader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=suspense-angst">suspense-angst</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1409174702" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1177357718578040509">It’s unconventional to want a man seven years older than you, a man who is your brother’s best friend. Lily, Luca’s baby sister, has always been in love with Jacob. It was the first kiss between her, 15, and Jacob, 22, that sealed their fate… As their paths continued to cross, they couldn’t deny the attraction they both shared. The forbidden nature of their love marked Lily’s age of transition and tested Jacob’s stamina. Their love was legally and morally wrong but Jacob was mature enough to sex</span>
  <span id="freeText1177357718578040509" style="display:none">It’s unconventional to want a man seven years older than you, a man who is your brother’s best friend. Lily, Luca’s baby sister, has always been in love with Jacob. It was the first kiss between her, 15, and Jacob, 22, that sealed their fate… As their paths continued to cross, they couldn’t deny the attraction they both shared. The forbidden nature of their love marked Lily’s age of transition and tested Jacob’s stamina. Their love was legally and morally wrong but Jacob was mature enough to sexually reject her when this was needed. In the beginning, a consensual relationship with young Lily seemed thrilling — but soon it only created gaps for self-doubt.<br><br>The relationship between them was exhilarating, drug-like…a warm secret humming in their chests. But, Lily was not of the age of consent and Jacob saw it as a double-edged sword. The man who promised to always be by her side, changed his mind and Lily was utterly devastated by his desire to leave.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1379.photobucket.com/user/Olga_NNikolaidi/media/raw_zpsghlrcded.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449694552ra/17325079.gif" alt=" photo raw_zpsghlrcded.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Now, he’s back in her life and wants to start fresh again. Any love worth having, is worth fighting for, and Jacob is willing to change for this woman and fight for her. Both of them are overpowered by love, but Lily isn’t emotionally ready enough to forgive him.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1379.photobucket.com/user/Olga_NNikolaidi/media/11962611_zpsrrbq2tfa.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449694552ra/17325080.gif" alt=" photo 11962611_zpsrrbq2tfa.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Jacob is invested in a life-changing-mind-blowing-heart-stopping-blood-rushing-difficult-but-extraordinary love with every bit of his heart. Will his relentless pursuit and strong feelings of love warm her?<br><br><br><a href="http://s1379.photobucket.com/user/Olga_NNikolaidi/media/12640700_zpskhgubnos.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449694552ra/17325081.gif" alt=" photo 12640700_zpskhgubnos.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>The author had me captivated from the start; you could feel the passion they had for each other from the beginning. They both cared for Luca, even denying the connection they both shared. It was great to read both characters’ POV’s. The story shows no matter the age gap between you and your partner, what’s truly important is you love each other. If you love a book with romance, passion, suspense and a little humour you will absolutely love this story! <br><br><i>ARC</i> kindly provided in exchange for an honest review.<br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5186551312316805206">I fell in love with the 1st book in The Good Ol' Boys series but I didn't enjoy this 2nd one much.<br/><br/>I have 2 main reasons for that and my 2 reasons are both about the hero, JACOB...<br/><br/>1. This book is about Jacob, one of the boys who tried hard to keep Alexandra and Lucas (heroine & hero in Book 1) apart, telling Lucas that she was their friend so they should all see her as their "sister" and she deserved someone better. But with the biggest hypocrisy, he fell for Lucas's baby-sister who is 7 years yo</span>
  <span id="freeText5186551312316805206" style="display:none">I fell in love with the 1st book in The Good Ol' Boys series but I didn't enjoy this 2nd one much.<br /><br />I have 2 main reasons for that and my 2 reasons are both about the hero, JACOB...<br /><br />1. This book is about Jacob, one of the boys who tried hard to keep Alexandra and Lucas (heroine &amp; hero in Book 1) apart, telling Lucas that she was their friend so they should all see her as their "sister" and she deserved someone better. But with the biggest hypocrisy, he fell for Lucas's baby-sister who is 7 years younger than him and all this thing started when she was 15 and he was 22.<br /><br />When Lucas learnt about their affair many years later, he said what I exactly thought:<br /><i>"After all the years and everything you did to keep Alex and I apart… you were fucking around with my baby sister? You’re such a goddamn hypocrite.” </i><br /><br />Yeah.. this is reason one! I never managed to forgive him for keeping my favorite people - Alex &amp; Lucas - apart, so I never cared about his happiness.<br /><br />2. My second reason is the age difference between him and Lily when it all started. I didn't mind it when she was 24 and he was 31 but I kind of was irritated when she was 15-16 and he was 22, 23...<br /><br />And Jacob's calling Lily "Kid" all the time didn't help it at all!<br /><br />Also, another boy in the group, Dylan, who became a police officer, said to Jacob: <i><br />“Always knew you liked little girls, I should arrest your sorry ass.”</i><br />Well, this didn't help at all, either. It just made me feel sick to my stomach again... <br /><br />So, that is my reason number 2 for not caring about this relationship. <br /><br />And when you don't care about the hero's happy end, no matter how well the book is written, you can't enjoy it much.<br /><br />If these two reasons do not bother you, it is a well-written book, you can go ahead and try. But, again, if you have read and loved Book 1, it is very hard to like this one for the obvious reasons...<br /><br />P.S. I really wonder what will happen in Book 3 to Dylan, another boy in the group. <br /><br />This second book contained vital information about the 3rd book, so if you are going to read Book 3, you should read Book 1 and Book 2 for the breadcrumbs the writer has left on the pages of the previous books.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7122259796805628594">I am a huge fan of forbidden romance so this one was right up my alley! And it was soooo good! I really enjoyed the first book in this series, <i>Complicate Me</i>, about Alex and Lucas, but I LOVED this one, the second book, <i>Forbid Me</i>, Lily and Jacob’s story.<br/><br/>Lily is Lucas’ little sister. Jacob is Lucas’ best friend. We met both of them in the first book and could already see the connection between the two. But, for years, the two fight their feelings for one another; it’s wrong, she’s too young, what </span>
  <span id="freeText7122259796805628594" style="display:none">I am a huge fan of forbidden romance so this one was right up my alley! And it was soooo good! I really enjoyed the first book in this series, <i>Complicate Me</i>, about Alex and Lucas, but I LOVED this one, the second book, <i>Forbid Me</i>, Lily and Jacob’s story.<br /><br />Lily is Lucas’ little sister. Jacob is Lucas’ best friend. We met both of them in the first book and could already see the connection between the two. But, for years, the two fight their feelings for one another; it’s wrong, she’s too young, what will others say. However, Lily is feisty and sassy and she gets what she wants.<br /><br /><b>“What are you inkling for? Mmm, you smell good enough to eat. Is that what you want me to do? Spread your legs like you know I love and taste your sweet pussy?”</b><br /><br />When the two finally can’t fight it anymore, it is HOT and intense. The connection between the two is like nothing else. They are each other’s lobsters.<br /><br /><b>“You’re mine. Only mine. Always been mine. Say what I need to hear.”</b><br /><br />I absolutely loved this book. I couldn’t put it down and read it in a matter of hours! I loved how it went back and forth between the past and present to give us the answers to all their complications. I adored how much of the other boys we got to see. I really enjoyed how we got to see parts from the first book from Jacob or Lily’s perspective. This book was sweet, sexy, emotional, and I want more. I am so excited for Dylan and Aubrey’s story next! ~ Tiffany, 5 stars<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1344483540678570818">So I finished it but only because the prologue gripped me and I wanted to find out what happened next. Forbidden romance and falling for your besties little sister are usually right up my street, but sadly it didn't quite live up to its early promise. <br/><br/> My issues for anyone interested:<br/><br/>I understood this could be read as a standalone even though it's the second in the series, but it wasn't really a standalone I'm afraid. I think I missed too much back story and character history to make sense of th</span>
  <span id="freeText1344483540678570818" style="display:none">So I finished it but only because the prologue gripped me and I wanted to find out what happened next. Forbidden romance and falling for your besties little sister are usually right up my street, but sadly it didn't quite live up to its early promise. <br /><br /> My issues for anyone interested:<br /><br />I understood this could be read as a standalone even though it's the second in the series, but it wasn't really a standalone I'm afraid. I think I missed too much back story and character history to make sense of the relationships in this. <br /><br />The then and now narrative combined with the alternating fp narrative messed with the flow of the story and confused me; admittedly, this was not helped by the fact that I hadn't read book one.<br /><br />The writing style jarred with me. I was pulled out of the story frequently by what seemed to me to be some pretty clunky phrases and language: "What are you inkling for?" and "'I thought we were going to eat' I seductively feigned" are a couple of examples but there were lots of others in a similar vein. It just sounded awkward to me.<br /><br />This is a complete story, but based on my experience, I'd definitely recommend reading the first book before reading this. <br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_1397110504" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1397110504" />
    <a title="Marci" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16735205-marci"><img alt="Marci" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1364659442p2/16735205.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1397110504?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marci" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marci" href="/user/show/16735205-marci">Marci</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1397110504" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15237365766541913042">M. Robinson manages to do it again... Another amazing story and another glimpse into The Good Ol' Boys Series. <br/><br/>In "Forbid Me" , book two of The Good Ol' Boys Series, we meet Jacob. Remember him, one of Lucas' biggest cock blockers in "Complicate Me"? He's the oldest of the good ol' boys, the bossy one. My, my, my how the tables have turned in "Forbid Me". <br/><br/>"Forbid Me" picks up where "Complicate Me" left off, however, both can be read as standalone novels. In "Forbid Me" we get a good look into Ja</span>
  <span id="freeText15237365766541913042" style="display:none">M. Robinson manages to do it again... Another amazing story and another glimpse into The Good Ol' Boys Series. <br /><br />In "Forbid Me" , book two of The Good Ol' Boys Series, we meet Jacob. Remember him, one of Lucas' biggest cock blockers in "Complicate Me"? He's the oldest of the good ol' boys, the bossy one. My, my, my how the tables have turned in "Forbid Me". <br /><br />"Forbid Me" picks up where "Complicate Me" left off, however, both can be read as standalone novels. In "Forbid Me" we get a good look into Jacob and Lily's relationship. NOW, what I LOVE, LOVE, LOVE, about M. Robinson's writing is that you meet her characters as youths. It's brilliant, because you are drawn in from the very beginning, relating and loving the characters. Even in their worst moments and worst behavior, you can't help but to sympathize with them. When you know where they've come from, you can almost justify their actions. Anyway, we meet Lily and Jacob at the tender ages of ten (Lily) and sixteen (Jacob), and how we meet them is HILARIOUS! (THIS IS A NO SPOILER ZONE, YOU'LL HAVE TO READ FOR YOURSELF) Lily is definitely crushing on her big brother's best friend, and constantly looking for every opportunity to impress him and be around him. Jacob is often times impressed, and dotes on her every chance he can get. He adores the little girl. He's nicknamed her KID. It's all very sweet and innocent. <br />As the book continues, and time progresses, these characters mature and feelings evolve into something that neither one them can fully handle. Actually, Jacob can't fully handle. (YOU'LL SEE WHEN YOU READ IT). There are some major obstacles standing in the way of their love and attraction for one another. For one, her age. Then there's that minor detail of her being his best friend's BABY sister. Through out "Forbid Me", there are other moments that deter these two to get it right and just be together.<br /><br />SO, I LOVE THIS SERIES.. I LOVE THIS BOOK... I LOVE THESE CHARACTERS!!!!!! First of all, "Forbid Me" took me thru so many emotions. I felt a sense of nostalgia, during parts of their childhood. Lily's innocence, but fresh ways, with her eaves dropping on the boys conversations, or her revealing her curiosity for kink with her movie choices. Lily's humor and snark also had me stitches. Like her mother and her book of Lily's made up words, I was ready to write down everything she said to Jacob. (LILY-ISMS) Her humor was infectious. The banter between she and Jacob seemed to be push and pull at times, but she knew how to bring Jacob to his knees, literally and figuratively. I loved it. Lily could be a pretty little liar at times, when it came to getting Jacob right where she needed him. I loved how he tried to resist her every time, but she proved to be stronger, in the their battle of wills. And when you thought she'd defeated him, he resorted to that alpha male behavior we all love and yearn for. I loved the anticipation, and the build up to every intimate scene, even when it resulted in them walking away from each other. The chemistry between these two was off the charts. "Forbid Me" has some extremely, panty soaking scenes (OR BEARD DRENCHING SCENES... WHICH EVER YOU CHOOSE) !!!!! <br />But, what is a M. Robinson novel, without a teary moment or two. While, I was not an emotional wreak through out the read, like I was with "Complicate Me", there are moments that pull at your heart strings, and make your throat all lumpy. REMEMBER, SHE'S MADE YOU LOVE THESE CHARACTERS. YOU LAUGH WHEN THEY LAUGH, LOVE WHEN THEY LOVE, AND DAMN IT, YOU WILL CRY WHEN THEY CRY. <br /><br />I received my arc 4 days ago and I have already read it twice. I am sure I'll read it at least one more time before book three is released. I am in love with these characters, this book, and the series thus far. 5 STARS FROM ME :-)</span>
  <a data-text-id="15237365766541913042" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11834731-michele-mcmullen?shelf=arc-beta">arc-beta</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1442384368" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18170358949518528209">Forbid Me is the second book in the Good Ol'Boys saga by M. Robinson. We the reader are finally given Jacob and Lily's Forbidden Love Story!<br/><br/>7 Years......that is the difference in our ages. I am too old for her. It is too much when we are young but now....Now we are adults and to hell with what people think...what Lucas thinks. I am going after what is mine. <br/>Jacob and Lily's existence has been intertwined their entire lives. He has protected, comforted, and supported her whenever she needed. He w</span>
  <span id="freeText18170358949518528209" style="display:none">Forbid Me is the second book in the Good Ol'Boys saga by M. Robinson. We the reader are finally given Jacob and Lily's Forbidden Love Story!<br /><br />7 Years......that is the difference in our ages. I am too old for her. It is too much when we are young but now....Now we are adults and to hell with what people think...what Lucas thinks. I am going after what is mine. <br />Jacob and Lily's existence has been intertwined their entire lives. He has protected, comforted, and supported her whenever she needed. He was always there...Jacob her rock, her friend, her hero. It was easy in the beginning she was a kid "his kid" his best friend Luca's little sister. <br />Lily began to grow into herself. She became curious, sassy and beautiful so beautiful that everyone took notice especially Jacob. She began to question her feelings for Jacob and even though shy and innocent wanted to explore them. <br />Jacob's struggle is evident on every page. He is lead by his heart but his mind soon wants him to believe what he feels is wrong....forbidden. I commend M for making me the reader feel that pain and struggle. It was so powerful and overwhelming. <br />Jacob and Lily know that with each interaction the bond between them strengthens, sealing their fate. The attraction is undeniable and will soon overcome them. Jacob realizes this and decides to make their choice for them. He walks away...away from Lily...away from temptation...away from love. He must sever the ties. <br />The hurt does not fade with time. They are now adults and Lily will not be easily won over. The vulnerability, trust and innocence have been replaced with hurt, heartbreak and sass. Her love for him has been tainted by his actions and words. The damage is done. Jacob is not easy swayed and knows that he has to bring his A game to win back what is his. Actions speak louder than words and he has his work cut out for him! <br />Jacob and Lily own this story. You the reader can't help but be swept up in this captivating tale of young love. I must say that Lucas had wormed his way into my heart in the first book but Jacob swept in captured and ran with it! His sweet, seductive, filthy mouth took me over the edge. He planned each action and word with precision to prove his love to Lily! <br />So get ready to be pulled in by their amazing story. Jacob and Lily need to be heard! <br />Hats off to you M. I have again fallen in love with your characters and their journey!! <br />I was a beta reader and provided an arc for an honest review!<br />~~Michele McMullen~~<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14543248021370051482">Too many "he was my core", "she was my core", to be followed by wishy-washiness. The h relentlessly pursues H, which is never a favorite trope of mine, and the H seems to respond well enough when h is in the room, but has no problem putting her out of mind when she is out of sight, moving on with his life (going to college, law school, dating, building his career) and there is zero evidence he is pining for her, aside from cheap words. The writing was unbearable to me. In just one paragraph, we </span>
  <span id="freeText14543248021370051482" style="display:none">Too many "he was my core", "she was my core", to be followed by wishy-washiness. The h relentlessly pursues H, which is never a favorite trope of mine, and the H seems to respond well enough when h is in the room, but has no problem putting her out of mind when she is out of sight, moving on with his life (going to college, law school, dating, building his career) and there is zero evidence he is pining for her, aside from cheap words. The writing was unbearable to me. In just one paragraph, we have the H's blood boiling, followed by him becoming a ticking bomb ready to explode, and finally, a victim to be burned at the stake. Other cliche metaphors and expressions abound. From the aforementioned "you are my core", to calling his body "a wonderland", or talking about how she draws him "like a month to a flame." Seriously? The cherry on top of this cake was H slut shaming not only girls in general but the h herself, when, at sixteen years old, he sees her at a nightclub, and remarks that she is dressed like a slut with a face full of makeup (makeup, you say??? Oh, the horror. The horror...) I can't even believe I made it halfway into this book. What was I thinking?</span>

<div id="review_1463870297" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1463870297" />
    <a title="Ashleyjo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33970054-ashleyjo"><img alt="Ashleyjo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466919724p2/33970054.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1463870297?book_show_action=true">Dec 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ashleyjo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ashleyjo" href="/user/show/33970054-ashleyjo">Ashleyjo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33970054-ashleyjo?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1463870297" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5214233516950899274">****4 1/2 Forbidden Love Stars****<br/><br/>I have to say that this book started out very strange and a little icky for me. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449630968ra/17317106.gif' width='250' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Stay with me, though, because it ends up being one of those romances that will have you clapping and smiling like a fool at the end;) <br/><br/><b> TMI </b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449630968i/17317107.gif' width='250' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I normally don't mind age gaps, but (initially) there are several things here that made my brain gasp, 'ooookay, I'm not so sure I want to know this shit'... <br/><br/>a) where he is seventeen to her ten-years-old and she is overhearing him talking about</span>
  <span id="freeText5214233516950899274" style="display:none">****4 1/2 Forbidden Love Stars****<br><br>I have to say that this book started out very strange and a little icky for me. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449630968ra/17317106.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Stay with me, though, because it ends up being one of those romances that will have you clapping and smiling like a fool at the end;) <br><br><b> TMI </b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449630968i/17317107.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I normally don't mind age gaps, but (initially) there are several things here that made my brain gasp, 'ooookay, I'm not so sure I want to know this shit'... <br><br>a) where he is seventeen to her ten-years-old and she is overhearing him talking about "eating pussy" and she fears for him thinking he is eating 'meow' cats. <br><br>b) where he is a 20-year-old adult comforting a scared 13-year-old child.<br><br>c) where a 14-year-old girl innocently jumps on his 21-year-old morning wood and they laugh it off as a friendly awkward moment and dub his penis, "his friend."<br><br>All of these 'then' moments are written in a non-creepy, innocent type of way, mind you! He isn't a perv, but I still don't think it was a good move to have this much info/ detailed scenes into the early years of a romance that's morally &amp; legally questionable... <br><br>It's difficult to have ^this^ detailed loving pseudo big brother type relationship described between a child and an adult and <br><b> THEN </b> have the same characters evolve and transition to a teen and adult romance without the reader having a little moral pause about it all, ya feel me? <br><br>Transitions...,<br><br>The first transition, which is a mild kiss, takes place when she is still very young- 15 to his 22. He knows it's wrong, and he removes himself. <br><br>The next transition takes place on her sixteenth birthday, and this kiss is much more heated. <br><br>From her being 16-17 and him being 23-24, things heat up to oral sex and an on again-off again hidden relationship. <br><br>Sexual intercourse doesn't take place until she's legal. <br><br>IMHO: I think the author should've either lessened the age gap, omitted the details of childhood scenes when she was so, so, so fucking young and he is in his late teens and early 20's, or held off completely on them kissing and so forth until she was a couple years older. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449630968i/17317108._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I eventually was able to move on from the age thing and go on to love the story because he is a really good guy and actually loves her, but, sadly, I imagine some readers reactions will be unmovable from the .. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394693142ra/8890803.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><b>Moving On </b> <br><br>Both MCs have a POV. Awesome! <br><br>This book goes back and forth between then and now, with each time line progressing forward independently till they meet and progress as one. <br><br>My romantic misgivings about the 'then' periods aside, the romance in the 'now' is cute as a button. Both time lines were technically very well done. It was easy to follow &amp; added a lot of layering and suspense to the story. I wasn't ever bored, and I never even skimmed a single page. <br><br><b>Characters </b> <br><br>I don't warm to Lily immediately. I often found her adolescent character childish, but then I REMEMBER SHE WAS A FUCKING KID! <br><br>Anyway, I love the tough, snarky, witty woman she is an adult;) She's a funny brand of hell on wheels;) I kept picturing a brown haired... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449630968ra/17317109.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>
<br><br>Him... <br><br> "That lip is going to fall off, Kid. Then what am I going to kiss? <br><br>Her... <br><br>"My ass."<br><br>
</blockquote> <br><br>Lol, feisty ;) <br><br>Jacob is funny, demanding, and stubborn as hell. I love how he just keeps showing up and either giving or taking shit away from her. And, oh, the panty melting shit that comes out of his mouth: <br><br><blockquote> <br><br>"The only reason I would leave you again, baby, would be to take you to another room and fuck you senseless."<br><br>"I want you in my bed, but I <i>need </i> you in my life." <br><br>"Hurting you is my biggest regret, loving you is my only redemption."<br><br>
</blockquote> <br><br>And the panty melting shit he does... <br><br><blockquote>
<br><br>Her... <br><br> "So this is what you're going to do for the rest of our lives? Leave when you want but when I try to, you're going to take my truck apart?"<br><br>Him... <br><br>"Look what it's done for your perspective. You're picturing our future together. That's a step in the right direction." <br><br>
</blockquote> <br><br>They were endearing characters that lit the pages afire when they were together and broke your heart when apart. <br><br><b> Storyline </b> <br><br>The blurb says this is a standalone within a series. Most of the time that means characters are featured and then maybe make guest appearances as secondary characters get their own stories, and you don't rally miss anything skipping about. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449630968ra/17317110.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This storyline is so woven, uhm complexly intertwined, perhaps, in the secondary character involvement that I really wish I would've started at book one to know them better and better catch the secondary dots floating around in the storyline. <br><br>The heart of this story is a romance taking bloom and working around impossible circumstances for 10 years... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443215890ra/16333750.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449630968ra/17317111.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449630968ra/17317112.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Of course, there's just so much more to it than that - from coming of age issues, the grey area between right and wrong, family dynamics, friendship, illness, etc.. It's really a book that you just have to read to appreciate. <br><br>The ending was beautiful and perfect! And, I can't wait to see WTF a secondary character gets arrested for in the final damn sentence of the book! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449630968i/17317113.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b> Final Thoughts </b> <br><br>Spoilers for OM/OW<br><br>For those concerned with ow/om, yes, both MC's have sexual relationships with people during separations. No cheating. Other relationships are insignificant to the MCs, are not written in any detail other than to say they existed, and there are no written sex scenes outside the MCs. <br><br>Trigger alerts - cancer &amp; intimacies w/ underage MC.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5214233516950899274" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Lily was a very sweet and likeable heroine. She was no doormat ..thank god. She truly loved Jacob with all her heart, but she also knew when enough was enough.<br /><br />4 stars from me :))</span>

  <span id="freeText2248495174069742740" style="display:none">I absolutely love The Good Ol' Boys!<br />The first book in the series left us right at a jaw dropping moment, so I wanted this one really bad!!<br />It did not disappoint!! Jacob and Lilly's story was awesome. They had a completely forbidden relationship on so many levels. Their being together was totally wrong but here I sat reading it rooting for them.         <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5092387666734494692">Wow could this book be anymore AMAZING!!! This maybe the best book I read in a long time!!! I am obsessed with M Robinson books but this surpasses them all by a landslide!! I. Could. Not. Put. It. Down. LITERALLY!!! This series just keeps getting better and better!<br/><br/>Jacob and Lily! LOVE them!! The depth of the feeling and emotions they had were surreal. They were sooo real and relatable! I felt every feeling and emotion they had. It was intense, powerful, full of angst, captivating, intrigued, fun</span>
  <span id="freeText5092387666734494692" style="display:none">Wow could this book be anymore AMAZING!!! This maybe the best book I read in a long time!!! I am obsessed with M Robinson books but this surpasses them all by a landslide!! I. Could. Not. Put. It. Down. LITERALLY!!! This series just keeps getting better and better!<br /><br />Jacob and Lily! LOVE them!! The depth of the feeling and emotions they had were surreal. They were sooo real and relatable! I felt every feeling and emotion they had. It was intense, powerful, full of angst, captivating, intrigued, funny, and sad. Each one giving you the feels. Sooo many points in this book I would stop and think wow this book can't get any better and honestly it did! It was gripping, compelling, and pulled at your heartstrings!! Literally AMAZING for lack of a better word.<br /><br />Lily she is sooo funny, stubborn, determined, beautiful, but young. She changed and grows tremendously throughout the book!! Parts of this book I literally felt the same way. It made her easily relatable. I made connections between my life and this story. Which to me only adds to how great this book truly is. She is 7 years younger then her brother Lucas's best friend Jacob. One of the Good Ol' Boys who she grew up surrounded by but, too young to be apart of the group. Jacob is alpha male, domineering, sexy, funny, and always trying to do the right thing. Torn between what's right and wrong. Being pulled and pushed back and forth. How such pain can they both go through and be put through before they make it? Or do you cut your losses and protect yourself?!<br /><br />This book is a whirlwind of a tornado that you can't help being sucked into.</span>

This book consumed my life from the first page until the end and yes I was still left wanting more!!   <span id="freeText17199776236248427379" style="display:none">Well it has happenend!!!! M.Robinson has outdone herself with Forbid Me!!! This book consumed my life from the first page until the end and yes I was still left wanting more!! This entire group of characters are absolutely amazing and suck you right into their lives!!!<br /><br />Jacob and Lily....what can I say?? I freaking loved them, every single thing about them. Although their relationship is not easy and of course they have so many different o sticles, you can not deny their attraction and chemistry. But is that really enough?<br /><br />I honestly can not say one bad thing about this book!! The writing was superb. It grabbed a hold of me and pulled me right in. The characters are flawless and have so many characteristics I love! The love, the chemistry, the wholy hotness was the perfect mixture. With just the right amount of drama and angst and of course our favorite, a hot alpha male, it was destined to be perfect! <br /><br />I would without a doubt recommend this book to everyone. I am dying for the next book in the series!!! This is definitely not only a book, but a series that will stay with me and is for sure one of my top favorites!!!!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('i+GkdQzcJ6RdJ1mv2kpUOMOmNcbXgvrkeLaRFFnZ2BEYgupziW8gRa2JNeSkjHCyl95DZthXjoUolF++C4QY+g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('S+PuQDzsptOon4HFTPVjCjzGXA896cUvRE4sbbOdjarYgKBGuV+hMlgx7Y4yM0eAaL4qrzI8sU4UbOLH4cBNQQ==')})
  }
//]]>

  <span id="freeText8466966906572792698" style="display:none">M. Robinson is the Wall Street Journal &amp; USA Today Bestselling Author crowned as the “Queen of Angst” by readers around the world. Dive into her visionary world that will take you on a rollercoaster ride of emotions and leave you wanting more. She writes everything from contemporary to suspense romance and is best known for her novel, El Diablo.<br /><br />When M isn’t in the cave writing her next epic love story, you will find her shopping and living on a boat in Florida with her real life pirate, her lobster, her husband Bossman. Sipping on Starbucks and hanging out with their two dogs, a German shepherd mix and a gordito Wheaten Terrier reading a good book. Or spending time with her family, who she is extremely close with. <br /><br />Above all, M loves her readers more than anything and loves to connect with them! She is on all social media platforms @authormrobinson but you will find her in her happy place the most. Her VIP Reader Group on Facebook or her second favorite happy place, Instagram. <br /><br />Stay connected!</span>
